<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a> (3282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> nominative singular <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">seignor</i>; <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:senior.html>senior</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senex</i>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:senior.html>senior</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:seigneur.html>seigneur</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seignior</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a></i><span class="serial-comma">,</span><span class="serial-and"> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:monsieur.html>monsieur</a></i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular <a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">sires</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">siring</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sired</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:transitive.html>transitive</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:male.html>male</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> procreate; <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:father.html>father</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:beget.html>beget</a>, impregnate.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">شَرَاب</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šarāb</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> ***sjamaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sjamaan.html>sjamaan</a> (23016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">шама́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šamán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Evenki_language" class="extiw" title="w:Evenki language">Evenki</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="evn">шама̄н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="evn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">şamān</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> mentioned <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> 1714:
</p>
<ul><li><b>1714</b>, Cornelis <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bruin.html>Bruin</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:reizen.html>Reizen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> Moskovie, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> Persie <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:indie.html>Indie</a></i>, publ. <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> Wetstein, Oosterwyk amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Gaete, <a href = vnd.unilang:page.html>page</a> 11.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sjees.html>sjees</a> (99837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:chaise.html>chaise</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjees.html>sjees</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjezen.html>sjezen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjees.html>sjeesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
